 Harsh Vardhan held a meeting

 Harsh Vardhan, air pollution has been adopted by adopting steps like preventing the burning of organic fuels and crops, better management of crop residues, spraying water on dusty roads, ways to protect dust from construction sites and burning of crops

 paryaavaran mantri ne kaha ki hamen centre sarkaar ke dwaara nirdhaarit deergh avadhi kii sabhi yojanaon ke lagu karne par dhyaan dena chahie

 shri krishna janmashtami kaa parv deshbhar main khushi or ullas ke saath manaaya jaataa he

 agar aapke ghar main bhi janmashtami kii taiyaariyaan ho rahi he or abhi tak mandir vaala hissaa nahin sajaayaa he to ye tips aapke liye bahut hi madadgaar sabit honge
 1
 mandir ko phulon se sajaaen

 2
 rang birange parde kharid len
 Cover the back of the temple with curtains of red, yellow, blue or golden color
 isse pichhlaa hissaa dhak bhi jayega or khubasurat bhi najar aayega
 3
 mogare kii maalaon ko bahari hisse par lagaaein
 This will keep the scent around the temple, that too for a long time
 4
 Cleaning the temple, paste some bright paper on the lower part
 iske baad bhagwaan kii murtiyon ko saaf karke ek kram main lagaaein

 puja se pehle hi prasad or puja kii baaki saamagree ko ek badi puja thali main sajaa len
 5
 kanhaiya ke liye kapadon kaa chayan acha hona chahie
